character_event = { #Crusade to free Jerusalem
	id = 1500
	picture = "event_crusades"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = exists value = PAPA }
		condition = { 
			type = not	
			value = { type = crusade } 
		}
		condition = {
			type = or
			condition = { type = papacy }
			condition = {
				type = and
				condition = { type = is_independent }
				condition = { type = not value = { type = county } }
				condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = excommunicated } }
				condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = heretic } }
				condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = sceptical } }
			}
		}
		condition = { 	type = religion value = catholic }
		condition = { 	type = province 
			province = 774 #Jerusalem
			condition = {
				type = and
				condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = catholic }}
				condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = orthodox }}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 1800
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = year value = 1075 } }
			factor = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = and
				condition = { type = year value = 1075 }
				condition = { type = not value = { type = year value = 1085 } }
			}
			factor = 0.3
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = papacy }
			factor = 0.01 #papal controller is most likely to call it
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = papacy  } }
			condition = { type = duchy }
			factor = 10 #a duke unlikely to call one
		}

		modifier = {
			condition = { 	type = province 
				province = 772 #Acre
				condition = {
					type = and
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = catholic }}
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = orthodox }}
				}

			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { 	type = province 
				province = 775 #Jaffe
				condition = {
					type = and
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = catholic }}
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = orthodox }}
				}
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {

				province = 776 #Hebron

					type = and
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = catholic }}

				}
			}
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { 	type = province 
				province = 764 #Antiocheia
				condition = {
					type = and
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = catholic }}
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = orthodox }}
				}
			}
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { 	type = province 
				province = 483 #Rhodes
				condition = {
					type = and
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = catholic }}
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = orthodox }}
				}
			}
			factor = 0.95
		}
		modifier = {

			factor = 0.95
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { 	type = province 
				province = 777 #Kerak
				condition = {
					type = and
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = catholic }}
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = orthodox }}

		modifier = {

				province = 725 #Irbio
				condition = {

			}
			factor = 0.95
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { 	type = province 
				province = 773 #Tiberias
				condition = {
					type = and
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = catholic }}
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = orthodox }}
				}
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { 	type = province 
				province = 778 #Monreal
				condition = {
					type = and
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = catholic }}
					condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = orthodox }}
				}
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}

		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = crusader }
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = zealous }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = martial_cleric}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = trait value = martial_cleric }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = piety value = 10 }
			}
			factor = 0.95
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = piety value = 25 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = piety value = 50 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = piety value = 100 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = stability value = 1 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = stability value = 2 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = stability value = 3 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = stability value = 0 } }
			factor = 1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = stability value = -1 } }
			factor = 1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = stability value = -2 } }
			factor = 1.1
		}

	}
	action_a = { # petition the pope to call a new crusade to free the holy city!
		ai_chance = 40
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = not value = { type = gold value = 2000 } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 2500 }
				factor = 0.25
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = not value = { type = piety value = 20 } }
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = not value = { type = prestige value = 20 } }
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = papacy }
				factor = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = or
					condition = { type = title value = PAPA }
					condition = { type = title value = TEMP }
					condition = { type = title value = HOSP }
					condition = { type = title value = TEUT }
					condition = { type = title value = U000 }
					condition = { type = title value = U001 }
					condition = { type = form_of_goverment value = knight_order }
				}
				factor = 0.100
			}
		effect = { type = crusade value = 774 } #Jerusalem
		effect = { type = piety value = 50 }
		effect = { type = prestige value = 50 }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 25
			effect = { type = add_trait value = zealous }
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 25
			effect = { type = add_trait value = crusader }
		}
	}
	action_b = { # help finance a crusade to free the holy city!
		ai_chance = 25
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 2500 }
				factor = 3
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = not value = { type = gold value = 2000 } }
				factor = 0.2
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = not value = { type = piety value = 50 } }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = not value = { type = prestige value = 50 } }
				factor = 2
			}
		effect = { type = crusade value = 774 } #Jerusalem
		effect = { type = gold value = -2000 }
		effect = { type = piety value = 100 }
		effect = { type = prestige value = 300 }
		effect = { type = add_trait value = crusader }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 75
			effect = { type = add_trait value = zealous }
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 25
			effect = { type = add_trait value = generous }
		}
	}
	action_c = { #let it stay in heathen hands
		ai_chance = 15
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 2000 }
				factor = 0.3
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = trait value = crusader }
				factor = 0.1
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = trait value = zealous }
				factor = 0.2
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = piety value = 50 }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = prestige value = 100 }
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = or
					condition = { type = title value = PAPA }
					condition = { type = title value = TEMP }
					condition = { type = title value = HOSP }
					condition = { type = title value = TEUT }
					condition = { type = title value = U000 }
					condition = { type = title value = U001 }
					condition = { type = form_of_goverment value = knight_order }
				}
				factor = 0.00001
			}
		effect = { type = piety value = -100 }
		effect = { type = prestige value = -200 }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = zealous }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = crusader }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 25
			effect = { type = add_trait value = sceptical }
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 10
			effect = { type = add_trait value = coward }
		}
	}
}

character_event = { #end the Jerusalem crusade - Jerusalem not in Christian hands
	id = 1501
	picture = "event_crusades"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = crusade }
		condition = { type = target value = 774 } #Jerusalem
		condition = { type = papacy }
		condition = {
       			type = province 
			province = 774 #Jerusalem
			condition = {
				type = and 
				condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = catholic } }
				condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_religion value = orthodox } }
			}
		}
	}

	id = 1502

				type = or

	}

			condition = { type = province value = 728 } #Damascus
			condition = { type = province value = 730 } #Palmyra

			condition = { type = province value = 763 } #Alexandretta
			condition = { type = province value = 764 } #Antiocheia

			condition = { type = province value = 757 } #Fammagusta
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 4000
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = or
				condition = { type = trait value = ecclesiastical_education }
				condition = { type = trait value = detached_priest }
				condition = { type = trait value = martial_cleric }
				condition = { type = trait value = mastermind_theologian }
				condition = { type = trait value = scholarly_theologian }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}

			condition = { type = province value = 764 }
			factor = 0.4
		}

			condition = { type = province value = 774 }
			factor = 0.4
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = crusader }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = zealous }
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = merciful }
			factor = 2
		}
		#Other modifiers?
		modifier = { # could be higher but this is a chance for reparation
			condition = { type = trait value = excommunicated }
			factor = 4
		}
		modifier = { # pope shouldn't ask heretic for this
			condition = { type = trait value = heretic } 
			factor = 100
		}

			condition = { type = trait value = sceptical }
			factor = 1.2
		}

			factor = 1.1
		}

			condition = { type = trait value = war_invalid } #Has shown his personal engagement
			factor = 0.8
		}

character_event = { #Crusade to free Roma
	id = 1550
	picture = "event_crusades"

	trigger = {
		condition = { 
			type = not	
			value = { type = crusade } 
		}
		condition = {
			type = or
			condition = { type = papacy }
			condition = {
				type = and

			condition = { type = trait value = merciful }
			factor = 1.5
		}

			condition = { type = trait value = just }
			factor = 1.25
		}

			factor = 1.25
		}

			factor = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = mastermind_theologian }
			factor = 1.25
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not
				value = { type = ruler_prestige value = 10 }
				}
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = ruler_diplomacy value = 8 }
			factor = 1.5
		}
		effect = { type = ruler_gold scale = -0.083 }
		effect = { type = prosperity value = -1 }
		effect = { type = peasant_loyalty value = -0.2 }
		effect = { type = burgher_loyalty value = -0.1 }
		effect = { type = clergy_loyalty value = 0.1 }
		effect = { type = clergy_power value = 0.1 }
		effect = { type = ruler_prestige value = -10 }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = religion value = catholic }
			effect = { type = ruler_piety value = 10 }
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 33
			effect = { type = add_province_effect value = looted }
		}
		effect = { # Revolt is really nasty, so lowered the chance to balance it with A
			type = random
			chance = 10
			effect = { type = add_province_effect value = revolt }
		}
	}

	action_c = { #I am a little too busy crusading to do that at the moment
		ai_chance = 20
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = heretic }
			factor = 2.5
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = excommunicated }
			factor = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = merciful }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = sceptical }
			factor = 1.5
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not
				value = { type = ruler_piety value = 25	}
				}
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = { # Less likely to pick non-converting option for crusade target
			condition = { type = province value = 199 }
			factor = 0.1
		}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = or
					condition = { type = demesne value = PAPA }
					condition = { type = demesne value = TEMP }
					condition = { type = demesne value = HOSP }
					condition = { type = demesne value = TEUT }
					condition = { type = demesne value = U000 }
					condition = { type = demesne value = U001 }
				}
				factor = 0.00001
			}
		effect = { type = noble_power value = -0.2 }
		effect = { type = ruler_piety value = -25 }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 50 #hard to guess how the pope will view your lack of zeal
			effect = { type = ruler_piety value = -50 }
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 20 #pope may declare anathema
			effect = { type = add_province_effect value = heretic }
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 5 #a province under weak guidance could revolt
			effect = { type = add_province_effect value = revolt }
		}
	}
}

	id = 1700

			condition = { type = target value = 802 } #Alexandria

character_event = { #My Lord, there is a Crusade to the Holy Land and yet you harbour a heathen in your court. The Pope has fobiddem this!

	id = 1751
	picture = "event_heretic"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = crusade }
		condition = {
			type = or
			condition = { type = target value = 774 } #Jerusalem
			condition = { type = target value = 764 } #Antioch
			condition = { type = target value = 802 } #Alexandria
			condition = { type = target value = 817 } #Tunis
			condition = { type = target value = 496 } #Byzantion
		}
		condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_child } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = religion value = catholic } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = religion value = orthodox } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = ecclesiastical_education } }
		condition = { type = age value = 10 }
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = excommunicated } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = heretic } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = sceptical } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = zealous } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = merciful } }
		}
		#temporary spam fix - definitely needs to be reworked for 1.06
		condition = { type = or
			condition = { type = ai }
			condition = { type = marshal }
			condition = { type = steward }
			condition = { type = chancellor }
			condition = { type = spymaster }
			condition = { type = chaplain }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {

	months = 12

	}

	action_a = { #You shall convert, or die!
		ai_chance = 60
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = ruler_csc
					condition = { type = or
						condition = { type = title value = PAPA }
						condition = { type = title value = TEMP }
						condition = { type = title value = HOSP }
						condition = { type = title value = TEUT }
						condition = { type = title value = U000 }
						condition = { type = title value = U001 }
						condition = { type = form_of_goverment value = knight_order }
					}
				}
				factor = 100
			}
		effect = { #courtier refuses to convert and doesn't survive the inquisition
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = death }
		}
		effect = { type = set_to_realm_religion } #if he survives, he converts
		effect = { #...but it might take a lot of persuasion
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = add_trait value = war_invalid }
			effect = { type = add_trait value = illness }
			effect = { type = health value = -3 }
		}
		effect = { #...and he also find it an emotionally grueling experience
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = add_trait value = stress_symptom }
		}
		effect = { #...and he probably won't appreciate the experience
			type = random
			chance = 75
			effect = { type = loyalty value = -0.5 }
		}
		effect = { type = trigger for = ruler value = 1754 }
	}
	action_b = { #You shall be banished from my realm!
		ai_chance = 35
		effect = { type = courtier_defect value = none }
		effect = { type = trigger for = ruler value = 1755 }
	}
	action_c = { #I reject the pope's authority to influence my court!
		ai_chance = 5
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = ruler_csc
					condition = { type = or
						condition = { type = title value = PAPA }
						condition = { type = title value = TEMP }
						condition = { type = title value = HOSP }
						condition = { type = title value = TEUT }
						condition = { type = title value = U000 }
						condition = { type = title value = U001 }
						condition = { type = form_of_goverment value = knight_order }
					}
				}
				factor = 0.001
			}
		effect = { type = trigger for = ruler value = 1756 }
	}
}

character_event = { #My Lord, there is a Crusade to the Holy Land and yet there is a heathen in your court. The Pope has fobiddem this!

	id = 1753
	picture = "event_heretic"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = crusade }
		condition = {
			type = or
			condition = { type = target value = 774 } #Jerusalem
			condition = { type = target value = 764 } #Antioch
			condition = { type = target value = 802 } #Alexandria
			condition = { type = target value = 817 } #Tunis
			condition = { type = target value = 496 } #Byzantion
		}
		condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_child } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = religion value = catholic } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = religion value = orthodox } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = ecclesiastical_education } }
		condition = { type = age value = 10 }
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = excommunicated } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = heretic } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = sceptical } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = zealous } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = trait value = merciful }
		}
		#temporary spam fix - definitely needs to be reworked for 1.06
		condition = { type = or
			condition = { type = ai }
			condition = { type = marshal }
			condition = { type = steward }
			condition = { type = chancellor }
			condition = { type = spymaster }
			condition = { type = chaplain }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {

	months = 24 

	}

	action_a = { #Escort the heathen from my realm!
		ai_chance = 60
		effect = { type = courtier_defect value = none }
		effect = { type = trigger for = ruler value = 1760 }
	}
	action_b = { #I tire of all these papal decrees!
		ai_chance = 5
		effect = { type = trigger for = ruler value = 1761 }
	}
	action_c = { #My court shall show no mercy towards heathens! Summon the Inquisador!
		ai_chance = 35
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = ruler_csc
					condition = { type = or
						condition = { type = title value = PAPA }
						condition = { type = title value = TEMP }
						condition = { type = title value = HOSP }
						condition = { type = title value = TEUT }
						condition = { type = title value = U000 }
						condition = { type = title value = U001 }
						condition = { type = form_of_goverment value = knight_order }
					}
				}
				factor = 1000
			}
		effect = { #courtier refuses to convert and doesn't survive the inquisition
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = death }
		}
		effect = { type = set_to_realm_religion } #if he survives, he converts
		effect = { #...but it might take a lot of persuasion
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = add_trait value = war_invalid }
			effect = { type = add_trait value = illness }
			effect = { type = health value = -3 }
		}
		effect = { #...and he also find it an emotionally grueling experience
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = add_trait value = stress_symptom }
		}
		effect = { #...and he probably won't appreciate the experience
			type = random
			chance = 75
			effect = { type = loyalty value = -0.5 }
		}
		effect = { type = trigger for = ruler value = 1762 }
	}
}

		}

			chance = 25

		}
	}
}

		effect = { type = remove_trait value = sceptical }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 33
			effect = { type = add_trait value = excommunicated }
		}
	}
}

	picture = "event_heretic"

		condition = { type = crusade }
		condition = {
			type = or
			condition = { type = target value = 181 } #Cordoba
			condition = { type = target value = 199 } #Burgos
		}
		condition = { type = region value = spain }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler_child } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = religion value = catholic } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = religion value = orthodox } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = ecclesiastical_education } }
		condition = { type = age value = 10 }
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = excommunicated } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = heretic } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = sceptical } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = zealous } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = merciful } }
		}
		#temporary spam fix - definitely needs to be reworked for 1.06
		condition = { type = or
			condition = { type = ai }
			condition = { type = marshal }
			condition = { type = steward }
			condition = { type = chancellor }
			condition = { type = spymaster }
			condition = { type = chaplain }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {

	months = 12 #should at least reduce the spam load from this event a little bit...

	}

	action_a = { #You shall convert, or die!
		ai_chance = 70
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = ruler_csc
					condition = { type = or
						condition = { type = title value = PAPA }
						condition = { type = title value = TEMP }
						condition = { type = title value = HOSP }
						condition = { type = title value = TEUT }
						condition = { type = title value = U000 }
						condition = { type = title value = U001 }
						condition = { type = form_of_goverment value = knight_order }
					}
				}
				factor = 100
			}
		effect = { #courtier refuses to convert and doesn't survive the inquisition
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = death }
		}
		effect = { type = set_to_realm_religion } #if he survives, he converts
		effect = { #...but it might take a lot of persuasion
			type = random
			chance = 60
			effect = { type = add_trait value = war_invalid }
			effect = { type = add_trait value = illness }
			effect = { type = health value = -3 }
		}
		effect = { #...and he also find it an emotionally grueling experience
			type = random
			chance = 60
			effect = { type = add_trait value = stress_symptom }
		}
		effect = { #...and he probably won't appreciate the experience
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = loyalty value = -0.5 }
		}
		effect = { type = trigger for = ruler value = 1854 }
	}
	action_b = { #You shall be bannished from my realm!
		ai_chance = 25
		effect = { type = courtier_defect value = none }
		effect = { type = trigger for = ruler value = 1855 }
	}
	action_c = { #I reject the Inquisition's authority to influence my court!
		ai_chance = 5
		effect = { type = trigger for = ruler value = 1856 }
	}
}

# A Zealous ruler converts another heathen #
############################################

character_event = { # My Lord, the Inquisador sends his compliments!

	id = 1858
	picture = "event_heretic"

	#triggered by 1852 action_b

	immidiate = {#Deus Vult!
		effect = { type = piety value = 10 }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 35
			effect = { type = gold value = 25 } # possible kick-back from the former heathen's estate
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 5
			effect = { type = add_trait value = cruel } #your actions might be misinterpreted as a little excessive
		}
	}
}

#######################################
# A zealous ruler's zeal is waivering #
#######################################

character_event = { # My Lord, that was a kind act!

	id = 1859
	picture = "event_heretic"

	#triggered by 1852 action_c

	immidiate = {#I suppose my zeal is waining!
		effect = { type = piety value = -20 }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = zealous }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = cruel }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = add_trait value = merciful }
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 20
			effect = { type = add_trait value = arbitrary } #your actions seem suspiciously arbirary
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 15
			effect = { type = add_trait value = sceptical } #and possibly even show a waivering of your faith
		}
	}
}

################################################
# A merciful ruler banishes a heathen courtier #
################################################

character_event = { # My Lord, the heathen has been escorted from the realm!

	id = 1860
	picture = "event_agriculture2" #seems like a nice and mercifully peaceful graphic to use

	#triggered by 1853 action_a

	immidiate = {#That is good!
		effect = { type = piety value = -5 }
		effect = { type = prestige value = 5 }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 20
			effect = { type = add_trait value = just }
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 5
			effect = { type = add_trait value = sceptical } #but could be view unfavourably by some
		}
	}
}

###########################################
# A merciful ruler tires of papal decrees #
###########################################

character_event = { # My Lord, you dare defy the Pope?!

	id = 1861
	picture = "event_heretic"

	#triggered by 1853 action_b

	immidiate = {#I suppose my faith is waining!
		effect = { type = piety value = -20 }
		effect = { type = add_trait value = sceptical }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 10
			effect = { type = add_trait value = stress_symptom } #this may have been a stressful decision
		}
	}
}

#################################################################
# A merciful ruler tires of showing mercy to wandering heathens #
#################################################################

character_event = { # My Lord, the Inquisador is pleased with your surprising change of heart!

	id = 1862
	picture = "event_heretic"

	#triggered by 1853 action_c

	immidiate = {#I suddenly feel so much more zealous!
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = merciful }
		effect = { type = add_trait value = zealous }
		effect = { type = piety value = 25 }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 35
			effect = { type = gold value = 25 } # possible kick-back from the former heathen's estate
		}
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 15
			effect = { type = add_trait value = cruel } #this may be viewed as a cruel and arbitrary act, considering you used to be so merciful
			effect = { type = add_trait value = arbitrary }
		}
	}
}

##########################################################################
# It can be dangerous to be a sceptic during the time of the Reconquista #
##########################################################################

character_event = { #My lord, the Inquisador has heard of your scepticism! He demands that you atone for your sins!

	id = 1863
	picture = "event_heretic"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = crusade }
		condition = {
			type = or
			condition = { type = target value = 181 } #Cordoba
			condition = { type = target value = 199 } #Burgos
		}
		condition = { type = ruler }
		condition = { type = region value = spain }
		condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
		condition = { type = trait value = sceptical }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = merciful } }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 48

		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = crusader }
			factor = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = piety value = 100 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = piety value = 500 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = piety value = 1000 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = intrigue value = 18 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = intrigue value = 15 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = intrigue value = 12 }
			factor = 1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = intrigue value = 8 } }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = intrigue value = 5 } }
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = intrigue value = 2 } }
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = piety value = 25 } }
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = piety value = 5 } }
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = piety value = 0 } }
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = piety value = 10 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = piety value = 50 }
			}
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = piety value = 100 }
			}
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = spymaster_csc
				condition = { type = intrigue value = 10 }
			}
			factor = 1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = spymaster_csc
				condition = { type = intrigue value = 14 }
			}
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = spymaster_csc
				condition = { type = intrigue value = 18 }
			}
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = liege
				condition = { type = trait value = zealous }
			}
			factor = 0.75
		}
	}

	action_a = { #I will beg the Pope's indulgence and atone for my sins!
		ai_chance = 50
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 50 }
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 100 }
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 500 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = or
					condition = { type = title value = PAPA }
					condition = { type = title value = TEMP }
					condition = { type = title value = HOSP }
					condition = { type = title value = TEUT }
					condition = { type = title value = U000 }
					condition = { type = title value = U001 }
					condition = { type = form_of_goverment value = knight_order }
				}
				factor = 100
			}
		effect = { type = gold scale = -0.75 }
		effect = { type = piety value = 25 }
		effect = { type = prestige value = -50 }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = sceptical }
	}

	action_b = { #I appeal the Inquisador's claim. I am no sceptic!
		ai_chance = 30
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 50 }
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 100 }
				factor = 1.5
			}
		effect = { type = gold scale = -0.25 } #court and bribery costs
		effect = { type = piety value = -10 }
		effect = { type = prestige value = 50 }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = sceptical }
		effect = { type = random_list
			35 = { type = no_effect }
			50 = { type = add_trait value = heretic }
			15 = { type = add_trait value = excommunicated }
		}
	}
	action_c = { #I defy the Inquisador to prove it!
		ai_chance = 20
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = not value = { type = gold value = 25 } }
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = not value = { type = gold value = 0 } }
				factor = 1.5
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 500 }
				factor = 0.1
			}
		effect = { type = piety value = -25 }
		effect = { type = prestige value = -50 }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = sceptical }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = add_trait value = excommunicated }
		}
	}
}

##################################################################################
# It is less dangerous to be a merciful sceptic during the time of a Reconquista #
##################################################################################

character_event = { #My lord, the Inquisador has heard of your scepticism! He demands that you atone for your sins!

	id = 1864
	picture = "event_heretic"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = crusade }
		condition = {
			type = or
			condition = { type = target value = 181 } #Cordoba
			condition = { type = target value = 199 } #Burgos
		}
		condition = { type = ruler }
		condition = { type = region value = spain }
		condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
		condition = { type = trait value = sceptical }
		condition = { type = trait value = merciful }
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 72

		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = crusader }
			factor = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = piety value = 100 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = piety value = 500 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = piety value = 1000 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = intrigue value = 18 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = intrigue value = 15 }
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = intrigue value = 12 }
			factor = 1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = intrigue value = 8 } }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = intrigue value = 5 } }
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = intrigue value = 2 } }
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = piety value = 25 } }
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = piety value = 5 } }
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = piety value = 0 } }
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = piety value = 10 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = piety value = 50 }
			}
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = chaplain_csc
				condition = { type = piety value = 100 }
			}
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = spymaster_csc
				condition = { type = intrigue value = 10 }
			}
			factor = 1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = spymaster_csc
				condition = { type = intrigue value = 14 }
			}
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = spymaster_csc
				condition = { type = intrigue value = 18 }
			}
			factor = 1.2
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = {
				type = liege
				condition = { type = trait value = zealous }
			}
			factor = 0.75
		}
	}

	action_a = { #I will beg the Pope's indulgence and atone for my sins!
		ai_chance = 50
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 100}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 500 }
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = or
					condition = { type = title value = PAPA }
					condition = { type = title value = TEMP }
					condition = { type = title value = HOSP }

					condition = { type = title value = U000 }
					condition = { type = title value = U001 }

	}

	action_b = { #I appeal the Inquisador's claim. I am no sceptic!
		ai_chance = 30
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = gold value = 25 }
				factor = 2
			}

				factor = 1.5
			}
		effect = { type = gold scale = -0.075 }
		effect = { type = piety value = -15 }
		effect = { type = prestige value = 20 }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = sceptical }

			50 = { type = no_effect }
			40 = { type = add_trait value = heretic }
			10 = { type = add_trait value = excommunicated }
		}
	}
	action_c = { #I defy the Inquisador to prove it!
		ai_chance = 20
			modifier = {
				condition = { type = not value = { type = gold value = 0 } }

}

###############################
# Ruler's children converted #
###############################

character_event = { #My child shall follow the same religion as I!

	id = 1865
	picture = "event_religion"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = crusade }
		condition = {
			type = or
			condition = { type = target value = 181 } #Cordoba
			condition = { type = target value = 199 } #Burgos
		}
		condition = { type = region value = spain }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = ruler } }
		condition = { type = ruler_child }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = religion value = catholic } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = religion value = orthodox } }
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = excommunicated } }
		}
		condition = { 
			type = ruler_csc
			condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = heretic } }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {

	days = 15 #should at least reduce the spam load from this event a little bit...

	}

	action_a = { #Christ is Great!
		effect = { type = set_to_realm_religion }
	}
}

## EXTRA CRUSADING TROOPS! ##
#############################

###################################################
# The peasants flock to support your Holy Crusade #
###################################################

character_event = {
	id = 1900

	picture = "event_mercenaries"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = ruler }
		condition = { type = crusade }
		condition = { type = on_crusade } #this can only happen if the target hasn't been captured yet and you're at war with the owner
		condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = excommunicated }}
		condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = heretic }}
		condition = { type = prestige value = 50 }
		condition = { type = capital
			condition = {
				type = and
				condition = { type = peasant_loyalty value = 0.75 }
				condition = { type = peasant_power value = 0.25 }
				condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 240

		# power and loyalty check
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = peasant_loyalty value = 0.85 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = peasant_loyalty value = 0.95 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = peasant_power value = 0.35 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = peasant_power value = 0.45 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = peasant_power value = 0.6 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}

		#capital province conditions check
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { looted = yes } }
			factor = 20
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { heretic = yes } }
			factor = 100
		}

			factor = 50

			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { typhoid_fever = yes } }
			factor = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { struggling = yes } }
			factor = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { poor = yes } }
			factor = 5
		}

			factor = 10

			factor = 1.25
		}

				condition = { type = title value = TEUT }
				condition = { type = title value = U000 }
				condition = { type = title value = U001 }
				condition = { type = form_of_goverment value = knight_order }
			}
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = not value = { type = realm_regiments value = 3 } }
			}
			factor = 0.05
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = stability value = 1 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = stability value = 2 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = stability value = 3 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = stability value = 0 } }
			factor = 1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = stability value = -1 } }
			factor = 1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = stability value = -2 } }
			factor = 1.1
		}
	}

	action_a = {#Deus Vult!
		effect = { 	type = add_regiment #this to default to the character's culture and capital province tech level
				strength = {
					militia = 500
					archers = 250
				}
		}
		effect = { 	type = add_regiment 
				strength = {
					militia = 400
				}
		}
#cost of this rem-ed out for now until the new effect is coded

						militia = 200
					}

	}

##################################################
# The burgers unite to support your Holy Crusade #
##################################################

character_event = {
	id = 1901

	picture = "event_crusades"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = ruler }
		condition = { type = crusade }
		condition = { type = on_crusade } #this can only happen if the target hasn't been captured yet and you're at war with the owner
		condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = excommunicated }}
		condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = heretic }}
		condition = { type = prestige value = 50 }
		condition = { type = capital
			condition = {
				type = and
				condition = { type = burgher_loyalty value = 0.75 }
				condition = { type = burgher_power value = 0.25 }
				condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 360

		# power and loyalty check
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = burgher_loyalty value = 0.85 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = burgher_loyalty value = 0.95 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = burgher_power value = 0.35 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = burgher_power value = 0.45 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = burgher_power value = 0.6 }
			}
			factor = 0.9
		}

		#capital province conditions check
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { looted = yes } }
			factor = 20
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { heretic = yes } }
			factor = 100
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { bubonic_plague = yes } }
			factor = 100
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { pneumonic_plague = yes } }
			factor = 100
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { malaria = yes } }
			factor = 20
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { dysentery = yes } }
			factor = 20
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { small_pox = yes } }
			factor = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { typhoid_fever = yes } }
			factor = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { struggling = yes } }
			factor = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { poor = yes } }
			factor = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { prosperous = yes } }
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_province_effect value = { rich = yes } }
			factor = 0.75
		}

		#ruler check
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = prestige value = 100 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = prestige value = 500 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = prestige value = 1000 }
			factor = 0.9
		}

			condition = { type = trait value = cruel }
			factor = 5
		}

			condition = { type = trait value = crusader }
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {

			factor = 0.9
		}

			condition = { type = trait value = generous }
			factor = 0.85
		}

			condition = { type = trait value = just }

		}

			condition = { type = trait value = sceptical }
			factor = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = selfish }
			factor = 1.25
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = vengeful }
			factor = 1.25
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = zealous }
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = amateurish_pettifogger }
			factor = 1.25
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = proven_dealbreaker }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = charismatic_negotiator }
			factor = 0.8

			factor = 0.75

			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {

			factor = 1.25
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = has_law value = { popular_law = yes } }
			factor = 0.75
		}

		#specific crusades modifiers
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = target value = 774 } #Jerusalem
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = target value = 764 } #Antioch
			factor = 0.85
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = target value = 802 } #Alexandria
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = target value = 817 } #Tunis
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = target value = 496 } #Byzantion
			factor = 0.75
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = target value = 333 } #Roma
			factor = 0.5
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = target value = 340 } #Sicily
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = region value = spain }
			condition = { type = target value = 181 } #Cordoba
			factor = 0.8
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = region value = spain }
			condition = { type = target value = 199 } #Burgos
			factor = 0.6
		}


		#difficulty setting modifiers
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = difficulty value = 3 }
			factor = 1.15
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = difficulty value = 4 }
			factor = 1.25
		}
		#special
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = or
				condition = { type = title value = PAPA }
				condition = { type = title value = TEMP }
				condition = { type = title value = HOSP }
				condition = { type = title value = TEUT }
				condition = { type = title value = U000 }
				condition = { type = title value = U001 }
				condition = { type = form_of_goverment value = knight_order }
			}
			condition = { type = capital
				condition = { type = not value = { type = realm_regiments value = 3 } }
			}
			factor = 0.05
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = stability value = 1 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = stability value = 2 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = stability value = 3 }
			factor = 0.9
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = stability value = 0 } }
			factor = 1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = stability value = -1 } }
			factor = 1.1
		}
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = not value = { type = stability value = -2 } }
			factor = 1.1
		}
	}

	action_a = {#Deus Vult!
		effect = { 	type = add_regiment #this to default to the character's culture and capital province tech level
				strength = {
					archers = 200 
					heavy_inf = 200 
					pikemen = 500 
				}
		}
		effect = { 	type = add_regiment 
				strength = {
					archers = 100 
					heavy_inf = 100 
					pikemen = 250 
				}
		}
#cost of this rem-ed out for now until the new effect is coded
#		effect = { type = prosperity for = capital value = -1 } #some of the troops come from your capital
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { 	type = add_regiment 
					strength = {
						heavy_inf = 100 
						pikemen = 250 
					}
			}
			effect = { 	type = add_regiment 
					strength = {
					pikemen = 250 
					}
			}
#			effect = { type = prosperity for = random value = -1 } #some come from the surrounding countryside
		}
	}

	action_b = {#I thank you, but I would prefer a financial contribution!
		effect = { type = prestige value = -10 }
		effect = { type = piety value = -10 }
		effect = { type = gold value = 200 }
		effect = {
			type = random
			chance = 33
			effect = { type = gold scale = 1 }
		}
	}
}

#######################################################
# Generate extra support for a liege who is crusading #
#######################################################

character_event = { #Your liege demands that you join the holy crusade.

	id = 1921
	picture = "event_crusades"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = is_vassal }
		condition = { type = religion value = catholic }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = atwar } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = excommunicated } }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = trait value = heretic } }
		condition = {
			type = realm_ruler
			condition = { type = and
				condition = { type = on_crusade }
				condition = { type = not value = { type = enemy_same_religion } }
			}
		}
		condition = { type = liege #to prevent vassals of player from DOWing...that's the player's decision
			condition = { type = ai }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 180
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = duchy }
			factor = 0.3
		}
	}

	action_a = { #I will summon my levies and follow the cross!
		ai_chance = 80
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = rebellious }
			factor = 0.1
		}
		effect = { type = relation for = liege value = 25 }
		effect = { type = declare_war value = crusade_target_owner }
		effect = { type = piety value = 15 }
		effect = { # possible enthusiastic response from your people
			type = random
			chance = 25
			effect = { type = add_regiment
				strength = {
					heavy_cav = 50 
					light_cav = 75 
					archers = 100 
					heavy_inf = 75 
					pikemen = 100 
					militia = 200
				}
			}
		}
	}
	action_b = { #No. I do not believe in this cause!
		ai_chance = 13
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = rebellious }
			factor = 0.5
		}
		effect = { type = relation for = liege value = -25 }
		effect = { type = piety value = -15 }
		effect = { type = add_trait value = heretic }
		effect = { type = loyalty value = -0.5 }
		effect = { #The pope will likely be pretty angry if he hears this
			type = random
			chance = 50
			effect = { type = add_trait value = excommunicated }
		}
	}
	action_c = { #No. I renounce my liege!
		ai_chance = 7
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = trait value = rebellious }
			factor = 100
		}
		effect = { type = trigger for = liege value = 6103 } # Notification, in realm_duress_events.txt
		effect = { type = piety value = -5 }
		effect = { type = independence }
		effect = { type = loyalty value = 1.0 }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = loyalist }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = rebellious }
		effect = { type = random_list
			50 = { type = add_trait value = reckless }
			30 = { type = add_trait value = deceitful }
			20 = { type = add_trait value = sceptical }
		}
		effect = { #the pope may not be impressed with your actions at this time
			type = random
			chance = 15
			effect = { type = add_trait value = excommunicated }
		}
	}
}

################################################################
# Vassals of Moslem rulers need support from their vassals too #
################################################################

character_event = { #The infidel has invaded my liege's realm!

	id = 1922
	picture = "event_muslim"

	trigger = {
		condition = { type = is_vassal }
		condition = { type = religion value = moslem }
		condition = { type = not value = { type = atwar } }
		condition = {
			type = realm_ruler
			condition = { type = on_crusade }
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 12
		modifier = {
			condition = { type = duchy }
			factor = 0.3
		}
	}

	action_a = { #I will summon my levies!
		ai_chance = 80
		effect = { type = relation for = liege value = 25 }
		effect = { type = declare_war value = crusade_target_owner }
		effect = { # possible enthusiastic response from your people
			type = random
			chance = 10
			effect = { type = add_regiment
				strength = {
					heavy_cav = 50 
					light_cav = 75 
					archers = 100 
					heavy_inf = 75 
					pikemen = 100 
					militia = 200
				}
			}
		}
	}
	action_b = { #Not my problem!
		ai_chance = 10
		effect = { type = relation for = liege value = -25 }
		effect = { type = loyalty value = -0.5 }
	}
	action_c = { #wOOt! Free at last!
		ai_chance = 10
		effect = { type = relation for = liege value = -100 }
		effect = { type = add_trait value = reckless }
		effect = { type = add_trait value = bastard } #simulates being cast out of family so can't inherit realm if liege's child
		effect = { type = independence }
		effect = { type = loyalty value = 1.0 }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = loyalist }
		effect = { type = remove_trait value = rebellious }
	}
}
